 bills through Mi Pay Payment App
 me pe (mi Pay) pement ap se dit (DTH) ko bhi richarge kar sakate hai

 agar aapke paas bhi shaomi (xiaomi) brands kaa phone he jo miyuai 10 par chalata he to aaie ham aapako Mi Pay ap ke bare main vistaar se jaankaree muhaiyaa karaate hai
 in Xiaomi smartphone, first of all you have to go to Mi App Store
 gaur karne vaali baat yah he ki Mi Pay ko is tarah se miyuai (MIUI) ke saath joda gaya he ki contact or esemes ap main bhi aapako send mani or transfar mani kaa vikalp nazar aayega
 After downloading and installing the app from the Mi App Store, log in with the Mi account running in the phone
 agar aapke paas me acount nahin he to aap creat bhi kar sakate hai
 After the app is set up, you can add your bank account by clicking on the bank account shown below in the app
 me pe ap ke jariye agar aap paise bhejnaa chaahate hai to aapako upar kii taraf 'transfar' (transfer) opshan dikhaai degaa

 agar aap paise bhejne vaale vyakti kii upiai idi se vaakif hai to pehle vikalp kaa chayan karen
 After entering the ID, click on the Next button shown below

 is vikalp par clic karne ke baad aapako sabase upar IFSC Code, bhejne vaale kaa naam, acount number or conform acount number main ditels bharani hongi
 Apart from this, if you want to go into the contact and click on the name of the person to whom you want to send money
 iske baad scrol karen yahaan aapako sidhe send mani kaa vikalp milegaa, is par clic karne ke baad aapke saamne phir se upar bataae gaye do vikalp khul jaaenge- 'send tu upiai idi' or doosraa 'send tu bank acount'
